#### Real-idx #0 (offset 366, 52 bytes)

- bytes  0..3  unknown(4): `83 07 00 00`

## `Learn` — TDEF page 519

- TDEF total bytes (after page-chain stitch): **4096**
- `num_cols` (offset 45, 2 bytes): **3**
- `num_idx` (offset 47, 4 bytes): **2**
- `num_real_idx` (offset 51, 4 bytes): **2**
- `ct_autonum` (Jet4 only, offset 28, 4 bytes): **0** — next ConceptualTableID for this table's complex columns
